MagikSF>
_block
    show("=== TODAS LAS COLECCIONES CON CAMPOS DE TODOS LOS DATASETS ===")

    _for ds _over gis_program_manager.cached_datasets()
    _loop
        _try
            show("")
            show("████ DATASET: ", ds, " ████")

            _for col_name _over ds.collections.keys.elements()
            _loop
                _try
                    col << ds.collection(col_name)
                    _if col _is _unset _then _continue _endif

                    reg << col.an_element()
                    _if reg _is _unset _then _continue _endif

                    show("  -- ", col_name)
                    _for campo _over reg.record_exemplar.all_fields.elements()
                    _loop
                        _try
                            val << reg.perform(campo.name)
                            _if val _isnt _unset
                            _then
                                show("      ", campo.name, " = ", val)
                            _endif
                        _when error
                        _endtry
                    _endloop
                _when error
                _endtry
            _endloop
        _when error
        _endtry
    _endloop
    show("=== FIN ===")
_endblock
